                <script type="text/javascript">

    function showHideSwitcher() {

        $('#CountryLangBodyWrapper').stop(true, true).toggle(function () {
            HandelHeaderTextToMatchDropDowns();
        });
        $('#CountryLangBodyWrapper input[type="submit"]').focusout(function () {
            //  $('#CountryLangBodyWrapper').hide();
            HandelHeaderTextToMatchDropDowns();
        });

        if ($('#CountryLangBodyWrapper').css('opacity') == '0') {
            $('#CountryLangHeaderWrapper').attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
        }
        else {
            $('#CountryLangHeaderWrapper').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
        }
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(document).mouseup(function (e) {
            var container = $("#languageSwitcher");
            var var2 = $("#CountryLangBodyWrapper");

            if (!container.is(e.target) // if the target of the click isn't the container...
                && container.has(e.target).length === 0) // ... nor a descendant of the container
            {
                var2.hide();
                HandelHeaderTextToMatchDropDowns();
                $('#CountryLangHeaderWrapper').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');

            }

        });

        $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_imgFlag').attr("alt", "");

        $(document)
            .keyup(function(e) {
                var container = $("#languageSwitcher");
                var var2 = $("#CountryLangBodyWrapper");
                if (!container.is(e.target) // if the target of the click isn't the container...
                    &&
                    container.has(e.target).length === 0) // ... nor a descendant of the container
                {
                    var2.hide();
                    HandelHeaderTextToMatchDropDowns();
                    $('#CountryLangHeaderWrapper').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');

                }

            });

        /* Switcher logic*/
        BindLanguageList();
        var hfLang = $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_HFSelectedLangId').val();
        if (hfLang != null && hfLang != '') {
            $('#dllLanguage').val(hfLang);
        }

        BindCountryLangText();

        $("#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_dllCountry").change(function () {
            BindLanguageList();
            BindHiddenFieldLangId();
        });
        $("#dllLanguage").change(function () {
            BindHiddenFieldLangId();
        });
    });

  
    function BindLanguageList() {
        // var LangIds = [];
        // var LangNames = [];
        /* store last selected value before clear dllLanguage*/
        var ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue = $('#dllLanguage option:selected').val();
        /*end*/
        $("#dllLanguage").html('');
        var ddlCountry = $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_dllCountry option:selected');
        var selectedCountryID = $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_dllCountry option:selected').val();
        var CountryLangString = $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_HFCountryLangJsonList').val();
        var CountryLangJsonList = JSON.parse(CountryLangString);
        var SelctedCountrLangList;

        // get List of languages for selected country
        $.each(CountryLangJsonList, function (key, value) {
            if (value.CountryId == selectedCountryID) {
                SelctedCountrLangList = value.LanguageList;
                
                return;
            }
        });

        // var attrs = ddlCountry[0].attributes;
        // var length = attrs.length;

        //for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        //    var attrName = attrs[i].name;
        //    if (attrName != 'value') {
        //        if (attrName.toLowerCase().indexOf("langid") >= 0) {
        //            LangIds.push(attrs[i].value);
        //        }
        //        else if (attrName.toLowerCase().indexOf("langname") >= 0) {
        //            LangNames.push(attrs[i].value)
        //        }
        //    }
        //}
        //$.each(LangIds, function (key, value) {
        //    $("#dllLanguage").append($("<option></option>").val(value).html(LangNames[key]));
        //});

        $.each(SelctedCountrLangList, function (key, value) {
            $("#dllLanguage").append($("<option></option>").val(value.LangId).html(value.LocalLanguageName).attr("lang", value.LanguageCode));
           // console.log(value.LangName);
        });

        // last selected languageid found on new langauge list
        if (ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue != null && ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue != '') {
            $.each(SelctedCountrLangList, function (key, value) {
                if (value.LangId == ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue) {
                    $('#dllLanguage').val(ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue);
                }
            });

        }

        // if (ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue != null && ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue != '' && $.inArray(ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue, LangIds) !== -1) {
        // $('#dllLanguage').val(ddlLanguageOptionselctedValue);
        //}
    }

    /// Bind lblCountryLang Text ///
    function BindCountryLangText() {
        var ddlLanguageOption = $('#dllLanguage option:selected');
        var ddlCountryOption = $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_dllCountry option:selected');
        var selectedLanguageText = ddlLanguageOption.text();
        var selectedCountryText = ddlCountryOption.text();
        var selectedLanguageID = ddlLanguageOption.val();
        var selectedCountryID = ddlCountryOption.val();
        var result = selectedCountryText + ' | ' + selectedLanguageText;
        var hiddenIds = selectedLanguageID + '#' + selectedCountryID;

        $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_lblCountryLang').text(result);
        $('#HFHeaderIds').val(hiddenIds);
    }

    // HFSelectedLangId Used in CodeBehind
    function BindHiddenFieldLangId() {
        var ddlLanguageID = $('#dllLanguage option:selected').val();
        $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_HFSelectedLangId').val(ddlLanguageID);
    }

    function HandelHeaderTextToMatchDropDowns() {
        var langId = $('#HFHeaderIds').val().split('#')[0];
        var countryId = $('#HFHeaderIds').val().split('#')[1];
        $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderTopHeader_PlaceHolderHeaderContent_Switcher_dllCountry').val(countryId);
        BindLanguageList();
        $('#dllLanguage').val(langId);
    }


</script>

                  <script type="text/javascript">
            //$(document).ready(function () {
            //main slider #myCarouselRevamp

            function toggleCarousel(thisBtn){
                //$("#myCarouselRevamp .carousel-pause-button").click(function () {
                if ($(thisBtn).hasClass('paused')) {
                    $(thisBtn).html('Carsouel is currently sliding click here to Pause it');
                    $('#myCarouselRevamp').data('bs.carousel').options.interval = 4000;
                    $("#myCarouselRevamp").carousel("cycle")
                }
                else {
                    $(thisBtn).html('Carsouel is currently paused  click here to slide through the items');
                    $('#myCarouselRevamp').data('bs.carousel').options.interval = 0;
                    $("#myCarouselRevamp").carousel("pause")

                }
                $(thisBtn).toggleClass('paused');
                return false;
            }
            //});


            //});

            // show modal function
            function showPopup(URLPath) {

                $('#homeBannerModal').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
                    $(this).find('iframe').attr('src', URLPath)
                });
                $('#homeBannerModal').modal({ show: true });

            }

            //Get Popup txt and append it to modal
            $(".HomeBannerPopUp").click(function () {
                $('#changedtxt').html($(this).children('span').html());
            });

            //Get Popup txt and append it to modal
            $(".HomeBannerPopUp").click(function () {
                var wpurl = $(this).children('span.changedUrl').html();
                $('#lnkPopupText').attr('href', wpurl);
            });

            // display modal
            $('.HomeBannerPopUp').click(function () {
                $('#popupText').modal({ show: true });
            });
            //close model after redirect
            $('#lnkPopupText').click(function () {
                $("#popupText").find(".close").click();
            });

    function checkAutoCompleteValidationBookingHP() {
        var bool;
        var fromList = document.querySelectorAll("[id*='txtFromCity']");
        var toList = document.querySelectorAll("[id*='txtToCity']");

        //for (var i = 0; i < fromList.length ; i++) {
        if (fromList[0].value.indexOf('(') > -1) {
            if (toList[0].value.indexOf('(') > -1) {
                bool = true;
            }
            else {
                bool = false;
                $("[id*='ucCountry_1_rfvTo']")[0].style.display = "block";
                return bool;
            }
        }
        else {
            bool = false;
            $("[id*='ucCountry_1_rfvFrom']")[0].style.display = "block";
        }

        // }
        return bool;
    }

    });

                      <script type="text/javascript">
    function showHideForBookingOnlineControls(selectedValue) {
        if (selectedValue == 'R') {
            if (($("[id*='txtFromCity']")[0].value.indexOf("(LHR)") > -1) || ($("[id*='txtToCity']")[0].value.indexOf("(LHR)") > -1)) {
                $('.londonChangeWidth').removeClass("col-sm-4").addClass("col-sm-3");
                $("[id*='youthDiv']").show();
            }
            else {
                $('.londonChangeWidth').removeClass("col-sm-3").addClass("col-sm-4");
                $("[id*='youthDiv']").hide();
            }

            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_rdtControl').style.display = 'block';
        }
        else if (selectedValue == 'O') {
            if (($("[id*='txtFromCity']")[0].value.indexOf("(LHR)") > -1)) {
                $('.londonChangeWidth').removeClass("col-sm-4").addClass("col-sm-3");
                $("[id*='youthDiv']").show();
            }
            else {
                $('.londonChangeWidth').removeClass("col-sm-3").addClass("col-sm-4");
                $("[id*='youthDiv']").hide();
            }
            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_rdtControl').style.display = 'none';
        }
        setOptionFunction('n');
    }

    var RBSchedule = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_RBSchedule');
    var RBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_RDPrice');
    var CKBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_chkFlexDate');
    var hiddenRBSchedule = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBSchedule');
    var hiddenRBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBPrice');
    var hiddenCBFlexPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenCBFlexPrice');
    var hiddenRBPriceDisabled = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBPriceDisabled');
    var hiddenHT = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenHT');
    var drpFareType = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFareType');
    var drpFlexPricer = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFlexPricer');

    function OnFareTypeItemsChanged(control) {
        debugger;
        var hiddenDrpFareTypes = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenDrpFareTypes');
        if (control.selectedIndex == 1) {
           
        }
        else if (control.selectedIndex == 2) {
            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_RBSchedule').checked = true;
            ChkSchedule(document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_RBSchedule'));
            //control.selectedIndex = 0;
            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFareType').selectedIndex = 1;
            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFlexPricer').selectedIndex = 0;
        }
        else {
            hiddenDrpFareTypes.value = control.options[control.selectedIndex].value;
        }
    }

    function ChkPrice(obj) {
        if (obj.checked) {
            var CKBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_chkFlexDate');
            var hiddenRBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBPrice');
            var hiddenRBSchedule = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBSchedule');

            CKBPrice.removeAttribute('disabled');
            CKBPrice.parentElement.removeAttribute('disabled');

            ShowHideDrpDowns(false, true);

            hiddenRBPrice.value = true;
            hiddenRBSchedule.value = false;
            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFlexPricer').selectedIndex = 0;
        }
    }

    function ChkSchedule(obj) {
        if (obj.checked) {
            var RBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_RDPrice');
            var CKBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_chkFlexDate');
            var hiddenRBSchedule = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBSchedule');
            var hiddenRBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBPrice');
            var hiddenCBFlexPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenCBFlexPrice');
            var hiddenRBPriceDisabled = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBPriceDisabled');

            CKBPrice.disabled = true;
            CKBPrice.checked = false;

            if (RBPrice.disabled)
                hiddenRBPriceDisabled.value = true;
            else
                hiddenRBPriceDisabled.value = false;

            ShowHideDrpDowns(true, false);

            hiddenRBSchedule.value = true;
            hiddenRBPrice.value = false;
            hiddenCBFlexPrice.value = false;
        }
    }

    function ChkFlexDates(obj) {
        var hiddenCBFlexPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenCBFlexPrice');

        if (obj.checked) {
            hiddenCBFlexPrice.value = true;
        }
        else {
            hiddenCBFlexPrice.value = false;
        }
    }

    function ShowHideDrpDowns(FareType, FlexPricer) {
        var drpFareType = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFareType');
        var drpFlexPricer = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFlexPricer');

        if (FareType) {
            drpFareType.style.display = 'block';
            drpFlexPricer.style.display = 'none';
        }
        else {
            drpFareType.style.display = 'none';
            drpFlexPricer.style.display = 'block';
        }
    }

    function FPMatchRoute(Load) {
        var Result = false;
        var arFPString = '';

        var fromcontrol = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucCountry_1' + '_txtFromCity');
        var tocontrol = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucCountry_1' + '_txtToCity');
        var RBSchedule = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_RBSchedule');
        var RBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_RDPrice');
        var CKBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_chkFlexDate');
        var hiddenRBSchedule = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBSchedule');
        var hiddenRBPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBPrice');
        var hiddenCBFlexPrice = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenCBFlexPrice');
        var hiddenRBPriceDisabled = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenRBPriceDisabled');
        var hiddenHT = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenHT');
        var drpFareType = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFareType');
        var drpFlexPricer = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_drpFlexPricer');
        var hiddenDrpFareTypes = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenDrpFareTypes');
        var hiddenDrpFareTypesItems = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_hiddenDrpFareTypesItems');

        var strFromAll = fromcontrol.value;
        var strToAll = tocontrol.value;

        if (strToAll != '') {
            var strFromArr = strFromAll.split("(");
            var strToArr = strToAll.split("(");

            var strFrom = strFromArr[1].split(")");
            var strTo = strToArr[1].split(")");

            var strFromTo = strFrom[0] + ',' + strTo[0];
            var strFromFrom = strTo[0] + ',' + strFrom[0];

            var arFPStrings = hiddenHT.value.split(";");

            for (i = 0; i < arFPStrings.length; i++) {
                arFPString = arFPStrings[i].split('|');

                if (arFPString[0].toLowerCase() == strFromFrom.toLowerCase()) {
                    Result = true;
                    break;
                }
                else if (arFPString[0].toLowerCase() == strFromTo.toLowerCase()) {
                    Result = true;
                    break;
                }
            }

            if (!Result) {
                RBPrice.checked = true;
                CKBPrice.checked = true;
                RBSchedule.checked = false;

                RBPrice.removeAttribute('disabled');
                CKBPrice.removeAttribute('disabled');

                if (RBPrice.parentNode.attributes['disabled'] != null && RBPrice.parentNode.attributes['disabled'].value == 'true') {
                    RBPrice.parentElement.removeAttribute('disabled');
                    CKBPrice.parentElement.removeAttribute('disabled');
                }

                hiddenRBSchedule.value = false;
                hiddenRBPrice.value = true;

                drpFareType.style.display = 'none';
                drpFlexPricer.style.display = 'block';

                //            for (i = (drpFlexPricer.options.length-1); i >= 0; i--)
                //            {
                //                drpFlexPricer.options[i]=null;
                //            }
                //            
                //            var drpItems = arFPString[1].split('-');
                //            for(i = 0; i < drpItems.length ; i++)
                //            {        
                //                var drpItem = drpItems[i].split('+');
                //                var option = document.createElement("OPTION");
                //                option.value = drpItem[1];
                //                option.text = drpItem[0];
                //                drpFlexPricer.options.add(option);
                //                
                //                hiddenDrpFareTypesItems.value = hiddenDrpFareTypesItems.value + drpItem[0] + '|' + drpItem[1] + ';';
                //            }

                //hiddenDrpFareTypesItems.value = hiddenDrpFareTypesItems.value.slice(0, hiddenDrpFareTypesItems.value.length -1);
                hiddenDrpFareTypes.value = drpFlexPricer.options[drpFlexPricer.selectedIndex].value;
            }
            else {
                RBSchedule.checked = true;
                RBPrice.disabled = true;
                CKBPrice.disabled = true;
                CKBPrice.checked = false;

                hiddenRBSchedule.value = true;
                hiddenRBPrice.value = false;
                hiddenCBFlexPrice.value = false;
                hiddenRBPriceDisabled.value = true;

                drpFareType.style.display = 'block';
                drpFlexPricer.style.display = 'none';

                hiddenDrpFareTypes.value = 'none';
            }
        }
    }
</script>

    // show modal function
    function showFindCityBookingPopup(URLPath) {

        var ucCountryId = URLPath.split('ucCountry_');
        var splittedId = ucCountryId[1];
        var modalId = splittedId.substr(0, 1);
        modalId = Number(modalId) - 1;

        $('.findCityBookingModal:eq(' + modalId + ')').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
            $(this).find('iframe').attr('src', URLPath)
        });
        $('.findCityBookingModal:eq(' + modalId + ')').modal({ show: true });
        /* 
         $('#findCityBookingModal').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
             $(this).find('iframe').attr('src', URLPath)
         });
         $('#findCityBookingModal').modal({ show: true });
         */

    }

    $("[id$=txtToCity]").keypress(function (event) {

        if (event.keyCode === 10 || event.keyCode === 13)
            event.preventDefault();

    });

    $("[id$=txtFromCity]").keypress(function (event) {

        if (event.keyCode === 10 || event.keyCode === 13)
            event.preventDefault();

    });

</script>

    if ($("[id$='nextMonth']") != null)
        $("[id$='nextMonth']").attr("title", "Next Month");
    if ($("[id$='prevMonth']") != null)
        $("[id$='prevMonth']").attr("title", "Previous Month");
    if ($("[id$='table']") != null)
        $("[id$='table']").attr("title", "Calendar");


    function PrepareDatePicker(SelectedDate, uc) {
        var vCalendarID = uc.id + "";
        var vDate1 = $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker('getDate');
        var vDate2;
        if (vCalendarID.match(/ucDepTime_1/gi)) {
            Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, uc.id);
            vCalendarID = vCalendarID.replace(/ucDepTime_1/gi, "ucReturnDate");
            vDate2 = $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker('getDate');
            $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker("option", "minDate", SelectedDate);
            if (vDate1 > vDate2) {
                Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, vCalendarID);
            }
        } else if (vCalendarID.match(/ucReturnDate/gi)) {
            Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, uc.id);
            //vCalendarID = vCalendarID.replace(/ucReturnDate/gi, "ucDepTime_1");
            //$("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker("option", "maxDate", SelectedDate);
        }
    }

    function Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, ucID) {
        if (SelectedDate == null) {
            //alert("No Date Selected");
        }
        else {
            var calenderName = ucID;
            var ucNameArr = calenderName.split("_");
            var n = 0;
            for (x in ucNameArr)
            { n = n + 1; }
            var ucName = calenderName.split("_", n - 1);
            var strUcName = ucName.toString().replace(/,/g, "_");
            //var lbldayName = strUcName.toString() + "_lblday";
            var lbldayName = ucID.replace(/_rdpCalender/gi, "_lblday");
            var gregorianDate = SelectedDate; //.getGregorianDate();
            var strGregorianDate = gregorianDate.toString();

            var Day = strGregorianDate.split(" ", 1);
            var FinalDay = strGregorianDate.split(" ", 1);

            var str = window.location.href;
            var pos = str.indexOf("Italian");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = 'lun';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = 'mar';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = 'mer';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = 'gio';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = 'ven';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = 'sab';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = 'dom';
            }


            pos = str.indexOf("German");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = 'Mo';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = 'Di';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = 'Mi';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = 'Do';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = 'Fr';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = 'Sa';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = 'So';
            }

            pos = str.indexOf("Chinese");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = '?';
            }


            pos = str.indexOf("Arabic");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = '???????';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = '????????';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = '????????';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = '??????';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = '??????';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = '?????';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = '?????';
            }

            pos = str.indexOf("Spanish");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = 'lun';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = 'mar';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = 'mié';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = 'jue';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = 'vie';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = 'sáb';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = 'dom';
            }

            pos = str.indexOf("French");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = 'Lun';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = 'Mar';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = 'Mer';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = 'Jeu';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = 'Ven';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = 'Sam';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = 'Dim';
            }

            if (document.getElementById(lbldayName) != null)
                document.getElementById(lbldayName).innerHTML = FinalDay;

        }
    }
</script>

                            <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    /*$(document).ready(function () {
        $('[data-toggle="popover"]').popover({ container: 'body' });
        //$("body").tooltip({
        //    selector: '[data-toggle=tooltip]',
        //    container: 'body'
        //});
    });*/
    window.setOptionFunction = function setOptions(type) {
       
        document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_youthVisibility').value = $("[id*='youthDiv']").is(":visible");

        var drpAdultName = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpAdult').selectedIndex;
        var drpChildName = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').selectedIndex;
        var drpYouthName = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').selectedIndex;
        var drpInfantName = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').selectedIndex;

        var childLength = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').length;

        var child = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').options[drpChildName].value;
        var adult = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpAdult').options[drpAdultName].value;
        var maxChildNum = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').options[childLength - 1].value;
        var maxYouthNum;


        if ($("[id*='youthDiv']").is(":visible")) {

            $("[id*='lblhint']").attr("data-original-title", '<ul><li>Card owner must be one of the traveller, holding his card while check in</li><li> You can book for up to 7 travellers and 7 infants at a time.</li><li> Youth, infants and children cannot travel alone and should be associated with an adult traveller. </li><li> Only one infant traveller per adult will be accepted.</li><li> Infant to 2 years old.</li><li> Child from 2 to 11 years old.</li><li> Youth from 12 to 16 years old.</li></ul>');
            if (type == 'c' || type == 'y' || (type == 'n' && child != 0)) {
                maxYouthNum = 7 -adult - child;
            }
            else
                maxYouthNum = 7 -adult;

            if ((maxChildNum <= maxYouthNum && (type == 'c' || type == 'y' || type == 'n')) || (type == 'y' && maxYouthNum <= maxChildNum)) {
                maxChildNum = 7 -adult - document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').options[drpYouthName].value;
                }
                else
                    maxChildNum = 7 -adult;
            }
            else {
                $("[id*='lblhint']").attr("data-original-title", '<ul><li>Card owner must be one of the traveller, holding his card while check in</li><li> You can book for up to 7 travellers and 7 infants at a time.</li><li> Infants and children cannot travel alone and should be associated with an adult traveller. </li><li> Only one infant traveller per adult will be accepted.</li><li> Infant to 2 years old.</li><li> Child from 2 to 11 years old.</li></ul>');
            maxChildNum = 7 -adult;

        }

        var maxInfantNum = adult;
        if ((type != 'c' && maxChildNum <= maxYouthNum) || (type == 'y' && maxChildNum >= maxYouthNum) || type == 'a') {
            var optLength = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').length;

            for (i = optLength; i > -1; i--) {
                document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').remove(i);
            }
            for (i = 0; i <= maxChildNum; i++) {
                var y = document.createElement('option');

                if (i == 0) {
                    var x = document.createElement('option');
                    x.text = '0 Child(ren)';
                    x.value = "0";
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').add(x, null)
                }
                else {

                    y.text = i.toString() + " " + 'Child(ren)';
                    y.value = i.toString();
                }
                try {
                    if (i != 0) {
                        document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').add(y, null);// standards compliant; doesn't work in IE
                    }
                }
                catch (ex) {
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').add(y); // IE only
                }
            }
        }
        if ($("[id*='youthDiv']").is(":visible") && type != 'y') {
            optLength = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').length;

            for (i = optLength; i > -1; i--) {
                document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').remove(i);
            }
            for (i = 0; i <= maxYouthNum; i++) {
                var y = document.createElement('option');
                if (i == 0) {
                    var x = document.createElement('option');
                    x.text = '0 Youth';
                    x.value = "0";
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').add(x, null)
                }
                else {
                    y.text = i.toString() + " " + 'Youth';
                    y.value = i.toString();
                }
                try {
                    if (i != 0) {
                        document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').add(y, null);// standards compliant; doesn't work in IE
                    }
                }
                catch (ex) {
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').add(y); // IE only
                }
            }
        }
        ///////Doesnt reset if its not adult
        if (type != 'y' && type != 'c') {
            optLength = document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').length;

            for (i = optLength; i > -1; i--) {
                document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').remove(i);
            }
            for (j = 0; j <= maxInfantNum; j++) {
                var y = document.createElement('option');
                if (j == 0) {
                    var x = document.createElement('option');
                    x.text = '0 Infant(s)';
                            x.value = "0";
                            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').add(x, null)
                        }
                        else {
                            y.text = j.toString() + " " + 'Infant(s)';
                            y.value = j.toString();
                        }
                        try {
                            if (j != 0) {
                                document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').add(y, null);// standards compliant; doesn't work in IE
                            }
                        }
                        catch (ex) {
                            document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').add(y); // IE only
                        }
                    }
                }

        if (type != 'a') {

            if (drpAdultName != 0) {
                if (drpAdultName == document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpAdult').length) {
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpAdult').selectedIndex = 0;
                }
                else {
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpAdult').selectedIndex = drpAdultName;
                }
            }
            if (drpChildName != 0) {
                if (drpChildName == document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').length) {
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').selectedIndex = 0;
                }
                else {
                    document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpChild').selectedIndex = drpChildName;
                }
            }
            if (drpYouthName != 0) {
                if (drpYouthName == document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').length) {
                     document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').selectedIndex = 0;
                 }
                 else {
                     document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpYouth').selectedIndex = drpYouthName;
                 }
             }
             if (drpInfantName != 0) {
                 if (drpInfantName == document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').length) {
                     document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').selectedIndex = 0;
                 }
                 else {
                     document.getElementById('ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_HomePageBooking1_ctl00_ucTraveler_drpInfant').selectedIndex = drpInfantName;
                 }
             }
         }

    }


</script>

                      <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">


    $("[id$=chkFlexDate]").keypress(function (event) {

        if (event.keyCode === 10 || event.keyCode === 13)
            event.preventDefault();

        if ($("[id$=chkFlexDate]").is(':checked')) {
            $("[id$=chkFlexDate]").prop('checked', false);
        } else {
            $("[id$=chkFlexDate]").prop('checked', true);
        }

    });

    $('input:checkbox[id$=chkFlexDate]').keydown(function (event) {

        if (event.keyCode === 10 || event.keyCode === 13)
            event.preventDefault();

        if ($("[id$=chkFlexDate]").is(':checked')) {
            $("[id$=chkFlexDate]").prop('checked', false);
        } else {
            $("[id$=chkFlexDate]").prop('checked', true);
        }

    });

    $("[id$=chkDirectFlight]").keypress(function (event) {

        if (event.keyCode === 10 || event.keyCode === 13)
            event.preventDefault();

    // show modal function
    function showFindCityBookingPopup(URLPath) {

        var ucCountryId = URLPath.split('ucCountry_');
        var splittedId = ucCountryId[1];
        var modalId = splittedId.substr(0, 1);
        modalId = Number(modalId) - 1;

        $('.findCityBookingModal:eq(' + modalId + ')').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
            $(this).find('iframe').attr('src', URLPath)
        });
        $('.findCityBookingModal:eq(' + modalId + ')').modal({ show: true });
        /* 
         $('#findCityBookingModal').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
             $(this).find('iframe').attr('src', URLPath)
         });
         $('#findCityBookingModal').modal({ show: true });
         */

    }

    if ($("[id$='nextMonth']") != null)

    function PrepareDatePicker(SelectedDate, uc) {
        var vCalendarID = uc.id + "";
        var vDate1 = $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker('getDate');
        var vDate2;
        if (vCalendarID.match(/ucDepTime_1/gi)) {
            Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, uc.id);
            vCalendarID = vCalendarID.replace(/ucDepTime_1/gi, "ucReturnDate");
            vDate2 = $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker('getDate');
            $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker("option", "minDate", SelectedDate);
            if (vDate1 > vDate2) {
                Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, vCalendarID);
            }
        } else if (vCalendarID.match(/ucReturnDate/gi)) {
            Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, uc.id);
            //vCalendarID = vCalendarID.replace(/ucReturnDate/gi, "ucDepTime_1");
            //$("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker("option", "maxDate", SelectedDate);
        }
    }

    function Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, ucID) {
        if (SelectedDate == null) {
            //alert("No Date Selected");
        }
        else {
            var calenderName = ucID;
            var ucNameArr = calenderName.split("_");
            var n = 0;
            for (x in ucNameArr)
            { n = n + 1; }
            var ucName = calenderName.split("_", n - 1);
            var strUcName = ucName.toString().replace(/,/g, "_");
            //var lbldayName = strUcName.toString() + "_lblday";
            var lbldayName = ucID.replace(/_rdpCalender/gi, "_lblday");
            var gregorianDate = SelectedDate; //.getGregorianDate();
            var strGregorianDate = gregorianDate.toString();

            var Day = strGregorianDate.split(" ", 1);
            var FinalDay = strGregorianDate.split(" ", 1);

            var str = window.location.href;
            var pos = str.indexOf("Italian");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = 'lun';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = 'mar';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = 'mer';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = 'gio';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = 'ven';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = 'sab';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = 'dom';
            }


            pos = str.indexOf("German");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = 'Mo';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = 'Di';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = 'Mi';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = 'Do';
                if (Day == 'Fri')
                    FinalDay = 'Fr';
                if (Day == 'Sat')
                    FinalDay = 'Sa';
                if (Day == 'Sun')
                    FinalDay = 'So';
            }

            pos = str.indexOf("Chinese");

            if (pos >= 0) {
                if (Day == 'Mon')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Tue')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Wed')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Thu')
                    FinalDay = '?';
                if (Day == 'Fri')

    function PrepareDatePicker(SelectedDate, uc) {
        var vCalendarID = uc.id + "";
        var vDate1 = $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker('getDate');
        var vDate2;
        if (vCalendarID.match(/ucDepTime_1/gi)) {
            Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, uc.id);
            vCalendarID = vCalendarID.replace(/ucDepTime_1/gi, "ucReturnDate");
            vDate2 = $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker('getDate');
            $("#" + vCalendarID).datepicker("option", "minDate", SelectedDate);
            if (vDate1 > vDate2) {
                Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, vCalendarID);
            }
        } else if (vCalendarID.match(/ucReturnDate/gi)) {
            Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, uc.id);
            //vCalendarID = vCalendarID.replace(/ucReturnDate/gi, "ucDepTime_1");

    function Calendar_OnDateSelected(SelectedDate, ucID) {

    function SendNotification(objID) {
        //debugger;
        var flightNumber = $("#" + objID).parent().parent().children("TD:eq(0)").html();
        var flightDate = $("#" + objID).next().html(); 
        var hdate = $("#" + objID).parent().parent().children("TD:eq(1)").html();
        var flightTime = $("#" + objID).parent().parent().children("TD:eq(2)").html();
        var flightFrom = $("#" + objID).parent().parent().children("TD:eq(4)").html();
        var flightTo = $("#" + objID).parent().parent().children("TD:eq(8)").html();
        var url = '/en/_layouts/LINKDev.EA.Portal.FlightStatus/flightstatusnotification.aspx?FNumber=' + flightNumber + '&FHDate=' + hdate + '&FDate=' + flightDate + '&FTime=' + flightTime + '&FFrom=' + encodeURI(flightFrom) + '&FTo=' + encodeURI(flightTo);

        $('#flightStatusNotification').on('show.bs.modal', function () { $(this).find('iframe').attr('src', url) });
        $('#flightStatusNotification').modal({ show: true });
    }


    $(document).ready(function () {
        $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip({ delay: { "hide": 2000 } });
        $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_g_0d874105_1e19_439d_ba0d_be7c65f55434_ctl00_txtFlightNo').keypress(function (e) {
            if (e.which == 13) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $('#ctl00_PlaceHolderMain_ctl00_Switcher_g_0d874105_1e19_439d_ba0d_be7c65f55434_ctl00_btnFind').click();
                //alert('You pressed enter!');
            }
        });
    });

                    <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function () {

        jQuery.fn.cleardefault = function () {
            return this.focus(function () {
                if (this.value == this.defaultValue) {
                    this.value = "";
                }
            }).blur(function () {
                if (!this.value.length) {
                    this.value = this.defaultValue;
                }
            });
        };
        jQuery(".txtMyBooking").cleardefault();

    });

    $("[id$=txtReservationNumber]").keypress(function (event) {

        if (event.keyCode === 10 || event.keyCode === 13)
            event.preventDefault();

    });

    $("[id$=txtLastName]").keypress(function (event) {

        if (event.keyCode === 10 || event.keyCode === 13)
            event.preventDefault();

    });

</script>

				else{
					//This Silde the silder by deafult if not USA					
                    $('.carousel-pause-button').trigger('click');

				}
				
				//Allow Aria Expanded Attr 
				$('.homeTabItem').click(function(){
					$('.homeTabItem > a').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
					$(this).find('a').attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
				});

				
            });  
            
           $(window).load(function () {
                var logoImages = document.getElementById('logo').getElementsByTagName('img');
            	logoImages[0].setAttribute('alt', 'EgyptAir, A StarAlliance Member');

				$('#searchContainer').remove();
				$(siteSearch).insertAfter('.newsHome')[0];
				var newsHome = $('.newsHome')[0];
				$(newsHome).css('display', 'inline-block')

            $(document).ready(function(){
            
             $("a[id*='CarsLink']").click(function () {
        	$('#CarRentalModel').modal({ show: true });
    	});
    	//close car model after redirect
         $("a[id*='lnkCarsPortal']").click(function () {
        	$("#CarRentalModel").find(".close").click();
    	});
        // display hotel modal
       $("a[id*='HotelsLink']").click(function () {
        	$('#HotelModel').modal({ show: true });
    	});
    	//close hotel model after redirect
         $("a[id*='lnkHotalPortal']").click(function () {
        	$("#HotelModel").find(".close").click();
    	});
		var x= $("#languageSwitcher span[id*='lblCountryLang']").text();
		if(x.toLowerCase().indexOf("united states") >= 0)
		{
			$('.sectionTitle').addClass('titleBackground');
			$('.wow').css('visibility', 'visible');
		}
		else{
			
				//animation
		        wow = new WOW(
		          {
		          boxClass:     'wow',      // default
		          animateClass: 'animated', // default
		          offset:       0,          // default
		          touch:       true,      
		          live:         true,       // default
		          mobile: false,
		          //scrollContainer: ".ms-backgroundImage"
		          scrollContainer: null

		        }
		        )
		        wow.init();
		    }
		$('#logo').find('img').attr('alt', 'EgyptAir, A StarAlliance Member');
	});
